IN PROGRESS:
- DX Style/Zed production-readiness goal remains active at an honest 89/100 for the source-only integration lane after the editor write-bridge preflight alignment checkpoint: source-only architecture and review gates are real, session tokens are UUID-backed, hidden from visible Web Preview URLs, reset on split, consumed only after trusted review, IPC queues have aggregate byte caps, native review revalidates trusted Web Preview packets against the stored generator-session source identity, and the request/session/live editor source must agree on path, structured byte span, active source length, bounded `fnv1a64:` digest, same-session source editor item/entity id, active buffer entity/remote id, multi-buffer id, worktree id, project path, singleton buffer kind, and a trusted dry-run structured edit preview scoped to the active source span with bounded replacement text. The DX Style editor write-bridge preflight now names those source/session/editor/dry-run/runtime proof gates as source-owned requirements while Zed copies them as review evidence. True 100/100 production readiness still needs authorized runtime/WebView/build proof and a mutation-capable editor write bridge; source mutation remains disabled.
- Latest source-write readiness checkpoint: DX Style's source-apply contract now names `source_write_readiness`, Zed's embedded mirror is synced, Web Preview copied review packets expose a redacted readiness object, native source-apply receipts preserve the same bounded readiness evidence, and refused/untrusted receipts fail closed with explicit missing requirements. This is still source-only evidence: Apply stays blocked, `can_mutate_source` remains false, and runtime/WebView/build proof plus a mutation-capable writer remain unproven.
- Latest reverse-delta effect slice: DX Style's reverse CSS delta contract now includes review-only value strategies for arbitrary shadow values, `drop-shadow(...)`, and `backdrop-filter: blur(...)`; Zed's Web Preview reverse-delta preview consumes those strategies for `box-shadow`, `text-shadow`, `filter`, and `backdrop-filter` output while preserving shadow color utilities and keeping source mutation disabled.
- Latest reverse-delta layout slice: DX Style's reverse CSS delta contract now covers layout/flex/grid review mappings for `align-items`, `justify-content`, `grid-template-columns`, `grid-template-rows`, `column-gap`, and `row-gap`; Zed Web Preview consumes the same strategy names so visual layout generator CSS can be reviewed as grouped atomics without enabling source writes.
- Latest reverse-delta spacing/sizing slice: DX Style's reverse CSS delta contract now covers deterministic `display`, `padding*`, `margin*`, `width`, `height`, `min-*`, `max-*`, and `align-content` mappings; Zed Web Preview consumes the same strategy names, including prefixless display utilities and negative-aware margin tokens, and keeps display as a fallback behind richer grid/flex declarations while source mutation remains disabled.
- Latest reverse-delta multi-strategy slice: DX Style and Zed now try all source-owned strategies for a supported declaration before refusing it, so real generator values such as pixel gaps, clamp padding, literal sizes, and pixel radii can fall back to arbitrary grouped atomics after token-specific mappings fail.
- Latest reverse-delta color-token slice: DX Style's reverse CSS delta contract now covers `outline-color`, `accent-color`, and `caret-color`; Zed Web Preview consumes the same mappings and preserves outline width/style utilities while reviewing outline color changes.
- Latest CSS hint alignment slice: DX Style's CSS declaration hint catalog and Zed's generated mirror now point `outline-color` at `outline-*` instead of `border-*`, keeping cursor-driven Style generator selection aligned with reverse-delta review.
- Latest reverse-delta transition slice: DX Style's reverse CSS delta contract now covers `transition-property`, `transition-duration`, `transition-delay`, and `transition-timing-function`; Zed Web Preview consumes the same strategy names so transition generator output can be reviewed as `transition-*`, `duration-*`, `delay-*`, and `ease-*` grouped atomics without enabling source writes.
- Latest easing metadata alignment slice: DX Style's easing/cubic-bezier generator catalog and CSS declaration hint catalog now route through `transition-timing-function` / `ease-*`, and Zed's generated mirrors carry the same source-owned metadata so cursor-driven generator selection matches the recipe output.
- Latest background-image reverse-delta slice: DX Style's reverse CSS delta contract now maps `background-image` to conservative `bg-[...]` review utilities, and Zed Web Preview uses a background-image-specific utility matcher so color tokens like `bg-primary` stay intact during gradient/image review.
- Latest shape/media reverse-delta slice: DX Style's reverse CSS delta contract now maps `clip-path` and `mask-image` generator output to `clip-path-[...]` and `mask-image-[...]`; Zed's generated reverse-delta mirror carries those source-owned mappings for Web Preview review.
- Latest transform reverse-delta slice: DX Style's reverse CSS delta contract now maps `transform` generator output to `transform-[...]`; Zed Web Preview uses a transform-specific family matcher so `rotate-*`, `scale-*`, and similar component utilities are preserved in review output.
- Latest background/border media reverse-delta slice: DX Style's reverse CSS delta contract now maps `background-size` and `border-image` to `bg-size-[...]` and `border-image-[...]`; broad `background` and `border` shorthands remain intentionally deferred.
- Latest animation reverse-delta slice: DX Style's reverse CSS delta contract now maps keyframe timeline `animation` output to `animate-[...]` for review, while DX-owned `@keyframes` source writing remains gated.
- Latest background shorthand reverse-delta slice: DX Style's reverse CSS delta contract now maps broad `background` output to conservative `bg-[...]` review utilities, preserving plain color tokens while replacing existing arbitrary/gradient background utilities.
